[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the Wireshark codebase [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing of the BER [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBasic Encoding Rules[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m dissector. The issue occurs in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_ber_GeneralString` function when processing crafted input, resulting in a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write beyond the bounds of a stack-allocated buffer named `name_string`. The[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability was identified through AddressSanitizer during fuzzing with the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandler_ber fuzzer.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **stack-buffer-overflow** vulnerability, specifically a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation that overflows a stack-allocated buffer. AddressSanitizer has assigned it[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma scariness score of [0m[1;36m46[0m[39m, indicating a moderate severity level for a [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Technical Details[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location of the Overflow:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow occurs at address `[0m[1;36m0x7ffd1684d15f[0m[39m` in the [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_ber_GeneralString` function at line [0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m34[0m[39m of [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-ber.c[0m[39m`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The write operation attempts to write [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte to a location that is outside the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds of the allocated buffer[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Buffer Information:**[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerable buffer is `name_string`, which is [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m bytes in size and allocated [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon the stack at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m160[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m240[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m within the `try_dissect_unknown_ber` function [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mframe[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The memory access occurs at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m, which is one byte before the start of the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_string` buffer, indicating an underflow rather than an overflow in the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraditional sense[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `name_string` buffer is declared at line [0m[1;36m825[0m[39m of packet-ber.c[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Call Stack:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered through the following call chain:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzzer entry point[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `epan_dissect_run` → [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `dissect_record` → [0m                                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Important Observations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Stack Frame Analysis:** The AddressSanitizer report shows the complete stack [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mframe of `try_dissect_unknown_ber`, which contains [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m objects. The memory access at[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m underflows the `name_string` variable, suggesting a possible off-by-one [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror or incorrect index calculation.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Shadow Memory Analysis:** The shadow byte at the problematic address shows [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`f2`, indicating a stack mid redzone [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpadding between stack variables[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirms that the write operation is accessing memory that should not be written [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto.[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Input:** The crash was triggered by a specific input sequence starting [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith bytes `[0m[1;36m0x1b[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x84[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0xc5[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x41[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x84[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0xc6[0m[39m`, followed by [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple `[0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m` bytes, and ending with `[0m[1;36m0x88[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m`.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Context:** The vulnerability occurs in the BER dissector while attempting to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissect unknown BER-encoded data, specifically when processing a GeneralString [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3178[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3179[0m[39m:    offset = [0m[1;35mdissect_ber_restricted_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse, BER_UNI_TAG_GeneralString, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactx, tree, tvb, offset, hf_id, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? &out_tvb : NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3180[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3181[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3182[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3183[0m[39m:         * XXX - do we want to just get what's left in the tvbuff[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3184[0m[39m:         * if the full length isn't available in the tvbuff, or[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3185[0m[39m:         * do we want to throw an exception?[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3186[0m[39m:         *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3187[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3188[0m[39m:            tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3189[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3190[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3191[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3192[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3193[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3194[0m[39m:            name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3195[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3196[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3197[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3198[0m[39m:    return offset;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3199[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability in `dissect_ber_GeneralString` has been [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclearly identified through the code analysis:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Issues[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Incorrect length retrieval [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m3188[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The function reads `tvb_len` from an[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary byte in the packet at the advanced offset position:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This is fundamentally wrong because:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It reads from the wrong tvbuff [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tvb` instead of `out_tvb`[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It reads at the wrong offset [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe advanced `offset` after parsing, not from [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe actual string content[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It treats arbitrary packet data as a length value[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Type mismatch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m3177[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: `tvb_len` is declared as `int8_t` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msigned [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-bit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut `tvb_get_uint8` returns an unsigned value [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m255[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. When the byte value is ≥[0m[1;36m128[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlike [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m in the fuzzer input[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it gets interpreted as a negative value [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0xff[0m[39m → [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Missing bounds validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m3194[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The null terminator placement uses [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe unvalidated `tvb_len` directly:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   When `tvb_len` is [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, this writes to `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, causing the underflow [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobserved at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mone byte before the buffer at offset [0m[1;36m160[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Correct Pattern[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase shows the correct pattern throughout [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-ber.c, packet-qsig.c, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket-dap.c, packet-x509if.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Use `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to get the actual parsed string length[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The old disabled version [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3040[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3101[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrates proper bounds checking: [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmax_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m len = max_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Replace incorrect length retrieval[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIn `epan/dissectors/packet-ber.c` at line [0m[1;36m3188[0m[39m, replace:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis retrieves the actual length of the parsed string data from the correct tvbuff,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing the established pattern used throughout the codebase.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Change variable type for safety[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAt line [0m[1;36m3177[0m[39m, change the type from `int8_t` to `unsigned`:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint8_t  tvb_len;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned tvb_len;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis prevents sign extension issues and matches the return type of [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Add bounds checking before null terminator placement[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBefore line [0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m, add validation to ensure `tvb_len` never exceeds the buffer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcapacity. The complete fixed section [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3187[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3195[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m should be:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        tvb_len = name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis ensures:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The null terminator is placed at most at index `name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindex [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m for an [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The copy operation respects buffer boundaries[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The logic matches the safe pattern from the old implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3091[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Simplify conditional logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39moptional cleanup[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe nested conditions at lines [0m[1;36m3189[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3193[0m[39m can be removed since the bounds checking [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis now done before the copy operation. The copy always uses the validated `tvb_len`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why this is optimal:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Follows established patterns**: Uses `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` like all [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother BER dissector functions in the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-ber.[0m[1;92mc:1803[0m[39m, [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket-qsig.[0m[1;92mc:2093[0m[39m, packet-dap.[0m[1;92mc:1543[0m[39m, packet-x509if.[0m[1;92mc:738[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Matches original safe implementation**: The bounds checking logic mirrors the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mold disabled version [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3091[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which had proper validation[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Minimal changes**: Only modifies the specific buggy lines without affecting [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe overall function structure or API[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Type safety**: Changing to `unsigned` prevents sign extension issues and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatches the return type of `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How it preserves existing logic:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Function signature unchanged**: The API remains the same, so all callers [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mtry_dissect_unknown_ber at line [0m[1;36m935[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to work[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Protocol parsing unaffected**: Still uses `dissect_ber_restricted_string` to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparse the BER encoding[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Tree structure maintained**: The proto_tree additions and dissection flow [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain identical[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How it addresses the issues:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fixes the overflow**: The bounds check ensures `tvb_len < name_len` before [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musing it as an index[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fixes the underflow**: Using unsigned type and proper length retrieval [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevents negative indices[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Correct data source**: Reads length from `out_tvb` which contains the actual [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsed string, not arbitrary packet data[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Prevents future issues**: The validation is explicit and matches the safe [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern used in the old implementation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential side effects and mitigation:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Truncated strings**: If the parsed string is longer than `name_len`, it will [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe truncated. This is intentional and matches the old implementation's behavior.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Null termination position**: The null terminator will always be placed within [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds, which may differ from previous behavior with malformed packets. This is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect - the old behavior was undefined/dangerous.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Test compatibility**: Existing tests should pass because well-formed packets [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill have string lengths that fit within typical buffer sizes. The fix only affects[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed packets that would have crashed before.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar solutions in codebase:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe old disabled implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3040[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3101[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrates the exact same [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds checking pattern at lines [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3091[0m[39m, confirming this is the intended [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproach for this dissector.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>epan/dissectors/packet-ber.[0m[1;92mc:3172[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3199[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
